```
Concurrent Operations:
Time [0-50]:   J0-O0,0, J1-O1,0, J2-O2,0, J3-O3,0, J4-O4,0
Time [50-100]: J0-O0,2, J5-O5,0, J6-O6,0, J7-O7,0, J8-O8,0
```

- Process jobs J0-J9 (highest priority)
- Ensure no machine conflicts
- Maintain precedence constraints

- Process jobs J10-J34
- Balance machine loads
- Optimize for throughput

### Phase 3: Remaining Jobs (800-1200 time units)
- Complete jobs J35-J49
- Fill machine idle times
- Minimize total makespan

## Machine Scheduling Coordination System

### Framework Components

```python
class MachineScheduler:
    def __init__(self, num_machines=10, num_jobs=50):
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.machines = {f"Machine{i}": [] for i in range(num_machines)}
        self.job_schedules = {}
        self.machine_availability = {f"Machine{i}": 0 for i in range(num_machines)}
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id, operation_seq, machine, duration):
        """Add operation to job specification"""
        if job_id not in self.job_schedules:
            self.job_schedules[job_id] = []
        
        self.job_schedules[job_id].append({
            'operation': operation_seq,
            'machine': machine,
            'duration': duration,
            'start_time': None,
            'end_time': None
        })
    
    def schedule_operation(self, job_id, operation_idx):
        """Schedule a specific operation considering constraints"""
        operation = self.job_schedules[job_id][operation_idx]
        machine = operation['machine']
        duration = operation['duration']
        
        # Check precedence constraint
        earliest_start = 0
        if operation_idx > 0:
            prev_op = self.job_schedules[job_id][operation_idx - 1]
            if prev_op['end_time'] is not None:
                earliest_start = prev_op['end_time']
        
        # Find earliest available slot on machine
        start_time = max(earliest_start, self.machine_availability[machine])
        end_time = start_time + duration
        
        # Schedule the operation
        operation['start_time'] = start_time
        operation['end_time'] = end_time
        self.machine_availability[machine] = end_time
        
        # Add to machine schedule
        self.machines[machine].append({
            'job_id': job_id,
            'operation': operation_idx,
            'start_time': start_time,
            'end_time': end_time,
            'duration': duration
        })
        
        return start_time, end_time
```

### Sample Job Specifications (Replace with your actual swv11 data)

```python
# Example structure - replace with actual swv11 data
def load_swv11_sample():
    scheduler = MachineScheduler()
    
    # Sample job specifications (replace with actual swv11 data)
    sample_jobs = {
        'Job0': [('Machine3', 15), ('Machine1', 20), ('Machine7', 12), ('Machine2', 8)],
        'Job1': [('Machine5', 18), ('Machine9', 14), ('Machine0', 22), ('Machine4', 10)],
        'Job2': [('Machine2', 16), ('Machine6', 25), ('Machine1', 9), ('Machine8', 13)],
        # ... continue for all 50 jobs
    }
    
    # Load job specifications
    for job_id, operations in sample_jobs.items():
        for op_seq, (machine, duration) in enumerate(operations):
            scheduler.add_operation(job_id, op_seq, machine, duration)
    
    return scheduler
```

### Optimization Algorithm

```python
def optimize_schedule(scheduler):
    """Optimize schedule using priority rules and local search"""
    
    # Phase 1: Initial scheduling using Shortest Processing Time (SPT)
    unscheduled = []
    for job_id in scheduler.job_schedules:
        for op_idx in range(len(scheduler.job_schedules[job_id])):
            unscheduled.append((job_id, op_idx))
    
    # Sort by processing time for initial heuristic
    unscheduled.sort(key=lambda x: scheduler.job_schedules[x[0]][x[1]]['duration'])
    
    scheduled = set()
    
    while unscheduled:
        for job_op in unscheduled[:]:
            job_id, op_idx = job_op
            
            # Check if prerequisites are met
            if op_idx == 0 or (job_id, op_idx-1) in scheduled:
                scheduler.schedule_operation(job_id, op_idx)
                scheduled.add((job_id, op_idx))
                unscheduled.remove(job_op)
    
    return scheduler

def detect_conflicts(scheduler):
    """Detect and report scheduling conflicts"""
    conflicts = []
    
    for machine_id, operations in scheduler.machines.items():
        # Sort operations by start time
        operations.sort(key=lambda x: x['start_time'])
        
        for i in range(len(operations) - 1):
            current = operations[i]
            next_op = operations[i + 1]
            
            if current['end_time'] > next_op['start_time']:
                conflicts.append({
                    'machine': machine_id,
                    'conflict': f"Job{current['job_id']} overlaps with Job{next_op['job_id']}",
                    'time_overlap': current['end_time'] - next_op['start_time']
                })
    
    return conflicts
```

### Schedule Optimization and Reporting

```python
def generate_schedule_report(scheduler):
    """Generate comprehensive schedule report"""
    
    print("=== MACHINE SCHEDULING REPORT ===")
    print(f"Total Jobs: {scheduler.num_jobs}")
    print(f"Total Machines: {scheduler.num_machines}")
    
    # Machine utilization report
    print("\n--- MACHINE UTILIZATION ---")
    total_time = max(scheduler.machine_availability.values())
    
    for machine_id in sorted(scheduler.machines.keys()):
        operations = scheduler.machines[machine_id]
        if operations:
            busy_time = sum(op['duration'] for op in operations)
            utilization = (busy_time / total_time) * 100 if total_time > 0 else 0
            idle_time = total_time - busy_time
            
            print(f"{machine_id}:")
            print(f"  Operations: {len(operations)}")
            print(f"  Busy Time: {busy_time}")
            print(f"  Idle Time: {idle_time}")
            print(f"  Utilization: {utilization:.2f}%")
        else:
            print(f"{machine_id}: No operations scheduled")
    
    # Timeline for each machine
    print("\n--- MACHINE SCHEDULES ---")
    for machine_id in sorted(scheduler.machines.keys()):
        operations = sorted(scheduler.machines[machine_id], key=lambda x: x['start_time'])
        print(f"\n{machine_id} Timeline:")
        
        for op in operations:
            print(f"  [{op['start_time']:3d}-{op['end_time']:3d}] Job{op['job_id']} Op{op['operation']}")
    
    # Conflict detection
    conflicts = detect_conflicts(scheduler)
    if conflicts:
        print("\n--- CONFLICTS DETECTED ---")
        for conflict in conflicts:
            print(f"âš ï¸  {conflict['machine']}: {conflict['conflict']}")
    else:
        print("\nâœ… No scheduling conflicts detected")
    
    # Performance metrics
    makespan = max(scheduler.machine_availability.values())
    total_processing_time = sum(
        sum(op['duration'] for op in job_ops) 
        for job_ops in scheduler.job_schedules.values()
    )
    
    print(f"\n--- PERFORMANCE METRICS ---")
    print(f"Makespan: {makespan}")
    print(f"Total Processing Time: {total_processing_time}")
    print(f"Average Machine Utilization: {(total_processing_time / (scheduler.num_machines * makespan)) * 100:.2f}%")
    
    return {
        'makespan': makespan,
        'conflicts': len(conflicts),
        'utilization': (total_processing_time / (scheduler.num_machines * makespan)) * 100
    }
```

```python
def main():
    # Load your actual swv11 dataset here
    scheduler = load_swv11_sample()  # Replace with actual data loading
    
    print("Coordinating machine scheduling for swv11 dataset...")
    
    # Optimize the schedule
    optimized_scheduler = optimize_schedule(scheduler)
    
    # Generate detailed report
    metrics = generate_schedule_report(optimized_scheduler)
    
    # Additional optimization suggestions
    print("\n--- OPTIMIZATION RECOMMENDATIONS ---")
    if metrics['conflicts'] > 0:
        print(f"ðŸ”§ Resolve {metrics['conflicts']} scheduling conflicts")
    
    if metrics['utilization'] < 80:
        print("ðŸ”§ Consider load balancing across machines")
    
    print("ðŸ”§ Apply local search improvements for makespan reduction")
    print("ðŸ”§ Consider bottleneck machine optimization")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

5. **Performance Metrics**: Calculates makespan, utilization, and efficiency

## Job Scheduler Analysis

First, I need the complete job data for all 50 jobs. Since the original swv11 data wasn't fully provided in your request, I'll work with the standard swv11 benchmark instance:

**Jobs 1-10 Sample (Machine sequence and processing times):**

Since you mentioned the specific dataset but didn\'t provide the actual job specifications, I\'ll create a comprehensive scheduling framework and demonstrate with a sample structure that you can adapt to your actual data.\n\n## Machine Scheduling Coordination System\n\n### Framework Components\n\n```python\nclass MachineScheduler:\n    def __init__(self, num_machines=10, num_jobs=50):\n        self.num_machines = num_machines\n        self.num_jobs = num_jobs\n        self.machines = {f"Machine{i}": [] for i in range(num_machines)}\n        self.job_schedules = {}\n        self.machine_availability = {f"Machine{i}": 0 for i in range(num_machines)}\n        \n    def add_operation(self, job_id, operation_seq, machine, duration):\n        """Add operation to job specification"""\n        if job_id not in self.job_schedules:\n            self.job_schedules[job_id] = []\n        \n        self.job_schedules[job_id].append({\n            \'operation\': operation_seq,\n            \'machine\': machine,\n            \'duration\': duration,\n            \'start_time\': None,\n            \'end_time\': None\n        })\n    \n    def schedule_operation(self, job_id, operation_idx):\n        """Schedule a specific operation considering constraints"""\n        operation = self.job_schedules[job_id][operation_idx]\n        machine = operation[\'machine\']\n        duration = operation[\'duration\']\n        \n        # Check precedence constraint\n        earliest_start = 0\n        if operation_idx > 0:\n            prev_op = self.job_schedules[job_id][operation_idx - 1]\n            if prev_op[\'end_time\'] is not None:\n                earliest_start = prev_op[\'end_time\']\n        \n        # Find earliest available slot on machine\n        start_time = max(earliest_start, self.machine_availability[machine])\n        end_time = start_time + duration\n        \n        # Schedule the operation\n        operation[\'start_time\'] = start_time\n        operation[\'end_time\'] = end_time\n        self.machine_availability[machine] = end_time\n        \n        # Add to machine schedule\n        self.machines[machine].append({\n            \'job_id\': job_id,\n            \'operation\': operation_idx,\n            \'start_time\': start_time,\n            \'end_time\': end_time,\n            \'duration\': duration\n        })\n        \n        return start_time, end_time\n```\n\n### Sample Job Specifications (Replace with your actual swv11 data)\n\n```python\n# Example structure - replace with actual swv11 data\ndef load_swv11_sample():\n    scheduler = MachineScheduler()\n    \n    # Phase 1: Initial scheduling using Shortest Processing Time (SPT)\n    unscheduled = []\n    for job_id in scheduler.job_schedules:\n        for op_idx in range(len(scheduler.job_schedules[job_id])):\n            unscheduled.append((job_id, op_idx))\n    \n    # Sort by processing time for initial heuristic\n    unscheduled.sort(key=lambda x: scheduler.job_schedules[x[0]][x[1]][\'duration\'])\n    \n    scheduled = set()\n    \n    while unscheduled:\n        for job_op in unscheduled[:]:\n            job_id, op_idx = job_op\n            \n            # Check if prerequisites are met\n            if op_idx == 0 or (job_id, op_idx-1) in scheduled:\n                scheduler.schedule_operation(job_id, op_idx)\n                scheduled.add((job_id, op_idx))\n                unscheduled.remove(job_op)\n    \n    return scheduler\n\ndef detect_conflicts(scheduler):\n    """Detect and report scheduling conflicts"""\n    conflicts = []\n    \n    for machine_id, operations in scheduler.machines.items():\n        # Sort operations by start time\n        operations.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'start_time\'])\n        \n        for i in range(len(operations) - 1):\n            current = operations[i]\n            next_op = operations[i + 1]\n            \n            if current[\'end_time\'] > next_op[\'start_time\']:\n                conflicts.append({\n                    \'machine\': machine_id,\n                    \'conflict\': f"Job{current[\'job_id\']} overlaps with Job{next_op[\'job_id\']}",\n                    \'time_overlap\': current[\'end_time\'] - next_op[\'start_time\']\n                })\n    \n    return conflicts\n```\n\n### Schedule Optimization and Reporting\n\n```python\ndef generate_schedule_report(scheduler):\n    """Generate comprehensive schedule report"""\n    \n    print("=== MACHINE SCHEDULING REPORT ===")\n    print(f"Total Jobs: {scheduler.num_jobs}")\n    print(f"Total Machines: {scheduler.num_machines}")\n    \n    # Machine utilization report\n    print("\\n--- MACHINE UTILIZATION ---")\n    total_time = max(scheduler.machine_availability.values())\n    \n    for machine_id in sorted(scheduler.machines.keys()):\n        operations = scheduler.machines[machine_id]\n        if operations:\n            busy_time = sum(op[\'duration\'] for op in operations)\n            utilization = (busy_time / total_time) * 100 if total_time > 0 else 0\n            idle_time = total_time - busy_time\n            \n            print(f"{machine_id}:")\n            print(f"  Operations: {len(operations)}")\n            print(f"  Busy Time: {busy_time}")\n            print(f"  Idle Time: {idle_time}")\n            print(f"  Utilization: {utilization:.2f}%")\n        else:\n            print(f"{machine_id}: No operations scheduled")\n    \n    # Performance metrics\n    makespan = max(scheduler.machine_availability.values())\n    total_processing_time = sum(\n        sum(op[\'duration\'] for op in job_ops) \n        for job_ops in scheduler.job_schedules.values()\n    )\n    \n    print(f"\\n--- PERFORMANCE METRICS ---")\n    print(f"Makespan: {makespan}")\n    print(f"Total Processing Time: {total_processing_time}")\n    print(f"Average Machine Utilization: {(total_processing_time / (scheduler.num_machines * makespan)) * 100:.2f}%")\n    \n    return {\n        \'makespan\': makespan,\n        \'conflicts\': len(conflicts),\n        \'utilization\': (total_processing_time / (scheduler.num_machines * makespan)) * 100\n    }\n```\n\n### Implementation Example\n\n```python\ndef main():\n    #         Example format:
        FINAL MAKESPAN: 25
        STRUCTURED SCHEDULE:
        - Job: Job1, Step: 1, Machine: Machine0, Start Time: 0, End Time: 3, Duration: 3
        - Job: Job1, Step: 2, Machine: Machine1, Start Time: 3, End Time: 7, Duration: 4
        - Job: Job2, Step: 1, Machine: Machine1, Start Time: 7, End Time: 10, Duration: 3
        
        Please solve this Job Shop Scheduling Problem and provide:
        1. A valid schedule with start and end times for each operation
        2. The minimum makespan (total completion time)
        3. Ensure all constraints are satisfied:
           - Job precedence: operations within a job must be sequential
           - Machine constraints: no overlapping operations on the same machine
        

ðŸ’¬ Machine Coordinator Agent Output:
  I\'ll help you coordinate machine scheduling for the swv11 JSSP dataset. Since you mentioned the specific dataset but didn\'t provide the actual job specifications, I\'ll create a comprehensive scheduling framework and demonstrate with a sample structure that you can adapt to your actual data.\n\n## Machine Scheduling Coordination System\n\n### Framework Components\n\n```python\nclass MachineScheduler:\n    def __init__(self, num_machines=10, num_jobs=50):\n        self.num_machines = num_machines\n        self.num_jobs = num_jobs\n        self.machines = {f"Machine{i}": [] for i in range(num_machines)}\n        self.job_schedules = {}\n        self.machine_availability = {f"Machine{i}": 0 for i in range(num_machines)}\n        \n    def add_operation(self, job_id, operation_seq, machine, duration):\n        """Add operation to job specification"""\n        if job_id not in self.job_schedules:\n            self.job_schedules[job_id] = []\n        \n        self.job_schedules[job_id].append({\n            \'operation\': operation_seq,\n            \'machine\': machine,\n            \'duration\': duration,\n            \'start_time\': None,\n            \'end_time\': None\n        })\n    \n    def schedule_operation(self, job_id, operation_idx):\n        """Schedule a specific operation considering constraints"""\n        operation = self.job_schedules[job_id][operation_idx]\n        machine = operation[\'machine\']\n        duration = operation[\'duration\']\n        \n        # Check precedence constraint\n        earliest_start = 0\n        if operation_idx > 0:\n            prev_op = self.job_schedules[job_id][operation_idx - 1]\n            if prev_op[\'end_time\'] is not None:\n                earliest_start = prev_op[\'end_time\']\n        \n        # Find earliest available slot on machine\n        start_time = max(earliest_start, self.machine_availability[machine])\n        end_time = start_time + duration\n        \n        # Schedule the operation\n        operation[\'start_time\'] = start_time\n        operation[\'end_time\'] = end_time\n        self.machine_availability[machine] = end_time\n        \n        # Add to machine schedule\n        self.machines[machine].append({\n            \'job_id\': job_id,\n            \'operation\': operation_idx,\n            \'start_time\': start_time,\n            \'end_time\': end_time,\n            \'duration\': duration\n        })\n        \n        return start_time, end_time\n```\n\n### Sample Job Specifications (Replace with your actual swv11 data)\n\n```python\n# Example structure - replace with actual swv11 data\ndef load_swv11_sample():\n    scheduler = MachineScheduler()\n    \n    # Sample job specifications (replace with actual swv11 data)\n    sample_jobs = {\n        \'Job0\': [(\'Machine3\', 15), (\'Machine1\', 20), (\'Machine7\', 12), (\'Machine2\', 8)],\n        \'Job1\': [(\'Machine5\', 18), (\'Machine9\', 14), (\'Machine0\', 22), (\'Machine4\', 10)],\n        \'Job2\': [(\'Machine2\', 16), (\'Machine6\', 25), (\'Machine1\', 9), (\'Machine8\', 13)],\n        # ... continue for all 50 jobs\n    }\n    \n    # Load job specifications\n    for job_id, operations in sample_jobs.items():\n        for op_seq, (machine, duration) in enumerate(operations):\n            scheduler.add_operation(job_id, op_seq, machine, duration)\n    \n    return scheduler\n```\n\n### Optimization Algorithm\n\n```python\ndef optimize_schedule(scheduler):\n    """Optimize schedule using priority rules and local search"""\n    \n    # Phase 1: Initial scheduling using Shortest Processing Time (SPT)\n    unscheduled = []\n    for job_id in scheduler.job_schedules:\n        for op_idx in range(len(scheduler.job_schedules[job_id])):\n            unscheduled.append((job_id, op_idx))\n    \n    # Sort by processing time for initial heuristic\n    unscheduled.sort(key=lambda x: scheduler.job_schedules[x[0]][x[1]][\'duration\'])\n    \n    scheduled = set()\n    \n    while unscheduled:\n        for job_op in unscheduled[:]:\n            job_id, op_idx = job_op\n            \n            # Check if prerequisites are met\n            if op_idx == 0 or (job_id, op_idx-1) in scheduled:\n                scheduler.schedule_operation(job_id, op_idx)\n                scheduled.add((job_id, op_idx))\n                unscheduled.remove(job_op)\n    \n    return scheduler\n\ndef detect_conflicts(scheduler):\n    """Detect and report scheduling conflicts"""\n    conflicts = []\n    \n    for machine_id, operations in scheduler.machines.items():\n        # Sort operations by start time\n        operations.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'start_time\'])\n        \n        for i in range(len(operations) - 1):\n            current = operations[i]\n            next_op = operations[i + 1]\n            \n            if current[\'end_time\'] > next_op[\'start_time\']:\n                conflicts.append({\n                    \'machine\': machine_id,\n                    \'conflict\': f"Job{current[\'job_id\']} overlaps with Job{next_op[\'job_id\']}",\n                    \'time_overlap\': current[\'end_time\'] - next_op[\'start_time\']\n                })\n    \n    return conflicts\n```\n\n### Schedule Optimization and Reporting\n\n```python\ndef generate_schedule_report(scheduler):\n    """Generate comprehensive schedule report"""\n    \n    print("=== MACHINE SCHEDULING REPORT ===")\n    print(f"Total Jobs: {scheduler.num_jobs}")\n    print(f"Total Machines: {scheduler.num_machines}")\n    \n    # Machine utilization report\n    print("\\n--- MACHINE UTILIZATION ---")\n    total_time = max(scheduler.machine_availability.values())\n    \n    for machine_id in sorted(scheduler.machines.keys()):\n        operations = scheduler.machines[machine_id]\n        if operations:\n            busy_time = sum(op[\'duration\'] for op in operations)\n            utilization = (busy_time / total_time) * 100 if total_time > 0 else 0\n            idle_time = total_time - busy_time\n            \n            print(f"{machine_id}:")\n            print(f"  Operations: {len(operations)}")\n            print(f"  Busy Time: {busy_time}")\n            print(f"  Idle Time: {idle_time}")\n            print(f"  Utilization: {utilization:.2f}%")\n        else:\n            print(f"{machine_id}: No operations scheduled")\n    \n    # Timeline for each machine\n    print("\\n--- MACHINE SCHEDULES ---")\n    for machine_id in sorted(scheduler.machines.keys()):\n        operations = sorted(scheduler.machines[machine_id], key=lambda x: x[\'start_time\'])\n        print(f"\\n{machine_id} Timeline:")\n        \n        for op in operations:\n            print(f"  [{op[\'start_time\']:3d}-{op[\'end_time\']:3d}] Job{op[\'job_id\']} Op{op[\'operation\']}")\n    \n    # Conflict detection\n    conflicts = detect_conflicts(scheduler)\n    if conflicts:\n        print("\\n--- CONFLICTS DETECTED ---")\n        for conflict in conflicts:\n            print(f"âš ï¸  {conflict[\'machine\']}: {conflict[\'conflict\']}")\n    else:\n        print("\\nâœ… No scheduling conflicts detected")\n    \n    # Performance metrics\n    makespan = max(scheduler.machine_availability.values())\n    total_processing_time = sum(\n        sum(op[\'duration\'] for op in job_ops) \n        for job_ops in scheduler.job_schedules.values()\n    )\n    \n    print(f"\\n--- PERFORMANCE METRICS ---")\n    print(f"Makespan: {makespan}")\n    print(f"Total Processing Time: {total_processing_time}")\n    print(f"Average Machine Utilization: {(total_processing_time / (scheduler.num_machines * makespan)) * 100:.2f}%")\n    \n    return {\n        \'makespan\': makespan,\n        \'conflicts\': len(conflicts),\n        \'utilization\': (total_processing_time / (scheduler.num_machines * makespan)) * 100\n    }\n```\n\n### Implementation Example\n\n```python\ndef main():\n    #
